fhi-align-direction-column-reverse--mobile">\n            <div class="fhi-col fhi-col-8@LG">\n                \n\n<div class="textual-block" data-auto-jumpto-index="">\n<h2 id="extract-from-daily-covid19-report-wednesday-29-april-2020"><strong><span style="font-size: 1.1em;">Extract from daily COVID-19 report - Wednesday 29 April 2020</span></strong></h2>\n<p>A status report is published every workday at 13:00, based on data from the Norwegian Surveillance System for Communicable Diseases (MSIS), microbiological laboratories, Norwegian Intensive Care Register and&nbsp;Norwegian Syndromic Surveillance System.</p>\n<ul>\n<li>Total of 7 667 people with confirmed COVID-19, of which 62 were reported yesterday. Updated on the 28.04.2020 at 24:00.</li>\n<li>202 deaths have been notified to the NIPH (as of 29.04.2020 at 08:00).&nbsp;</li>\n<li>A total of 169 124 have been tested for coronavirus (SARS-CoV-2) (as of 28.04.2020 at 15:00).&nbsp;</li>\n</ul>\n<h3>Intensive care patients</h3>\n<p>A total of 213 people in intensive care with confirmed coronavirus (SARS-CoV-2) have been treated in intensive care units, of these, 49 are inpatients. The average age of the 213 confirmed patients is 61 years, and 74 % are male. 30 deaths have been reported.</p>\n<p><em>(figures from Norwegian Intensive Care Register as of 29.04.2020 at 08:00.)</em></p>\n<h3>Laboratory analyses&nbsp;</h3>\n<p>The number of laboratory analyses with analyses results are now collected from the National Laboratory database. Analyses results reported on the testing date are copied from laboratories that test for SARS-CoV-2 directly to the database.</p>\n\n\n<!-- basic Highcharts block template -->\n<figure calculates the total mortality in Norway through the&nbsp;<a href="/sv/influensa/influensaovervaking/overvakingssystem-for-dodelighet-eu/">NorMOMO</a>-system. The status for total mortality is mentioned in the weekly reports.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><a href="https://www.euromomo.eu/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Latest diagram for European countries in EuroMOMO</a><br><br></li>\n</ul>\n<h3>Daily reproduction number - R</h3>\n<p>The modelling group at NIPH publishes daily reports with situational analyses and forecasting. The reports also include the latest calculation of the reproduction number, R, which shows how many people are infected by an infected person on average.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><a href="/en/id/infectious-diseases/coronavirus/coronavirus-modelling-at-the-niph-fhi/" target="_top">Coronavirus modelling at NIPH</a> - see pdf reports at the bottom of the page, table 1 in the report
